< review>
Smallcakes OC is the best and my most favourite cupcake shop ever! Love everything about it.

Starting from its location! Who wouldn‚Äôt love to grab a box and relax by the ocean while enjoying delicious cupcakes. I love how the store looks from the outside, extremely inviting, with it‚Äôs cute exterior! This place looks all the more adorable and gives a very cozy feeling when one goes inside. Every wall of Smallcakes is just so perfectly instagram-able!

A wide variety of cupcakes are so beautifully laid out in front of you , which makes it all the more tempting! The cake portion of the cupcake is as moist and flavourful as it can get with the frosting as perfect. I got an assorted box of 12, and I absolutely loved all the flavours, especially the chocolate cream which was so decadent, moist and sinful (but definitely worth sinning on). I wanted to truly indulge on dessert that day, so I thought I would give the ‚ÄúSmallcakes smash‚Äù a try, and boy I didn‚Äôt regret it one bit. It was a treat to my taste buds and a gastronomical delight. It‚Äôs a divine combination of their in house home made ice cream, sandwiched between gourmet cupcakes!

They even undertake customs orders for cupcakes, mini cupcakes and cakes. I love their cupcakes so much that I had mini pink and white cupcakes for an event during my wedding celebrations earlier and I‚Äôm going to get some for my best friends bridal shower coming up soon. To make things more exciting, they come up with a special and new cupcake creation every day of the week!

Even the packaging of the cupcake boxes is so well done! A big shoutout to their Instagram page which is always kept so interesting and always makes me eat with eyes first and then keeps me wanting to  come back for more. Also Small cakes didn‚Äôt forget about your pets,  who would love you all the more, for giving them their ‚Äúpup cake‚Äù treats! To allow you to give into your temptations and cupcake cravings, they even bring Smallcakes to your doorstep, via Grubhub, DoorDash, Uber eats and Postmates! I love their website, which is so tastefully done, has a detailed list of their signature cupcake options and icecream flavours for you to choose from.

Last but not the least, the owners are one of the most  warm, pleasant and professional people I have come across. They definitely add a personal touch to the whole Smallcakes experience.

A balanced diet is a cupcake in both hands.
Money can‚Äôt buy happiness but it can definitely buy cupcakes, and that‚Äôs pretty much the same thing!

Small cakes OC, you are certainly ‚ÄúBAKING THE WORLD A BETTER PLACE ONE CUPCAKE AT A TIME.‚Äù <3</review>

<UserId.>108002671681378609833<//UserId.><username>Arthur Wong< /username><date>1406846574665<//date><rate>5<//rate>< Review>
4 stars? hmm.. i think not. a definite 5 star restaurant. The outside of this restaurant is not compelling or attracting. But that shouldn't matter much if you seek some really good Mandarin Cuisine. You enter this old building and inside looks really huge. The high ceilings is something you wouldn't have expected. The restrooms are old school. I would suggest to update it a bit. "Old school" meaning it doesn't look like your modern restroom at a restaurant. The feel of the restaurant is nice. The menu is broad with many choices. This is the only place that makes the best mongolian beef. The beef with broccoli is pretty good. i would suggest beef with broccoli over rice with extra sauce. The main attraction to eat here is the fish filet. I would order fish in tangerine sauce and have it over rice with extra sauce. the tangerine sauce is definitely to die for. However, if you want to try-out this place first, I would suggest doing the lunch menu and come here for the cheaper and more affordable prices.<//Review>

< Text>
This is my first time eating "Vegan" pizza. Now, before any it's-solo-a-large-or-be-quiet pizza lovers try to come for my neck, if you see the small pizza in person, you can see it is a full pizza, even so in the pictures, the pizza is a decent size. I'm not much of a shopper, so take this review with a grain of salt - but I was a bit disappointed. I came for a bra, and while the gal who helped me was very sweet, the inventory was a mess. < Review>
This Macy's had really poor staff when I visited on a Weekday. Associates in the Men's dept, told us that sleeve alterations cost different amounts depending on how much you needed hemmed, the watch counter lady actually told me that the $189 watches were solid gold. The selection of clothes is decent, the prices are competitive, it seems that the quality of service is really poor for Macy's standards. Without a lot of competition in Fresno, it seems all too often that there is no incentive to improve the customer service.</Review>
